16 trait IntEncodersImplicits extends Serializable {
17 
18   // RuleResultWithProcessor's are lost in serialization by design, they only make sense in a given run
19 
20   /**
21    * Converts the DQ results to and from Int and RuleResult's.  Probability is processed by the value / PassedInt
22    */
23   implicit val ruleResultToInt: Injection[RuleResult, Int] = Injection(
24     {
25       case r: RuleResult => Serializing.ruleResultToInt(r)
26     },
27     {
28       case SoftFailedInt => SoftFailed
29       case DisabledRuleInt => DisabledRule
30       case FailedInt => Failed
31       case PassedInt => Passed
32       case a: Int => Probability(a.toDouble / PassedInt)
33     })
34 
35 }
36 
37 object IntEncoders extends IntEncodersImplicits {
38 }
39 
40 trait IdEncodersImplicits extends Serializable {
41   implicit val versionedIdNotNullable = new NotCatalystNullable[VersionedId] {}
42 
43   // try just id first
44   implicit val versionedIdTo: Injection[VersionedId, Long] = Injection(
45     {
46       case Id(id, version) => ((id.toLong) << 32) | (version & 0xffffffffL)
47     },
48     {
49       case a: Long =>
50         PackId.unpack(a)
51     })
52 }
53 
54 object IdEncoders extends IdEncodersImplicits {
55 
56 }

115 object EmptyMap extends MapData {
116   override val keyArray: ArrayData = new org.apache.spark.sql.catalyst.util.GenericArrayData(Array.empty)
117   override val valueArray: ArrayData = new org.apache.spark.sql.catalyst.util.GenericArrayData(Array.empty)
118   override def numElements(): Int = 0
119 
120   override def copy(): MapData = this
121 
122   override def toString: String = {
123     s"keys: $keyArray, values: $valueArray"
124   }
125 }
126 
127 object MapUtils {
128   def toScalaMap(map: MapData, keyType: DataType, valueType: DataType): Map[Any, Any] = {
129     val keys = map.keyArray.toObjectArray(keyType)
130     val values = map.valueArray.toObjectArray(valueType)
131     keys.zip(values).toMap
132   }
133 
134   /**
135    * Assuming MapData entries are stable, as they are array backed, over a dataset.  When the position of 'what' is not in the cachedPositions a full search is performed with the new location being returned in addition.
136    *
137    * @param mapData the source mapdata to search through.
138    * @param cachedPositions already known positions to check for what
139    * @param what compared against the keyArray to obtain the position
140    * @param getValue obtain the value from the mapData, with any necessary conversions, against the index parameter
141    * @tparam T
142    * @return (result from getValue or null when not found, either cachedPositions or cachedPositions and a newly found position)
143    */
144   def getMapEntry[T <: AnyRef](mapData: MapData, cachedPositions: Seq[Int], what: Any)(getValue: Int => T): (T, Seq[Int]) = {
145     val keys = mapData.keyArray()
146     val n = keys.numElements()
147     val acc = (idx: Int) => keys.getLong(idx)
148 
149     def search() = {
150       var i = 0
151       var found = false
152       while (i < n && !found) {
153         if (acc(i) == what) {
154           found = true
155         } else {
156           i += 1
157         }
158       }
159       if (!found)
160         -1
161       else
162         i
163     }
164 
165     def withCached() =
166       cachedPositions.find { i =>
167         if (i < n)
168           acc(i) == what
169         else
170           false
171       }
172 
173     withCached().map(i => (getValue(i), cachedPositions))
174       .getOrElse {
175         val r = search()
176         if (r == -1)
177           (null.asInstanceOf[T], cachedPositions)
178         else
179           (getValue(r), cachedPositions :+ r)
180       }
181   }
182 
183 }
